CREATE TABLE `message_medicalconditions` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `transactionInId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `sourceId` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'This is the id that the message source might have assigned to the record. For example, CCR components always has a CCRDataObjectId',
  `sourceDateType` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'The date type that the is provided with the record. It can be a date range, exact date, approximate date range, approximately age range, age range, verification date etc. ',
  `sourceDate` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'The date that the is provided with the record. e.g. exact time - Nov 11, 2011 11:11AM, age range - age 19-25',
  `conditionTypeId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'this will define if it is a problem in ccr - values could be diagnosis',
  `conditionId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'id from lu_MedicalConditions table',
  `conditionDate` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'The date that the is provided with the record for the condition. It could be different from SourceDate as sourceDate can be a range of when the patient is follow and conditionDate is when this medical condition happened. It can be a date range, exact date, approximate date range, approximately age range, age range, etc. e.g. exact time - Nov 11, 2011 11:11AM, age range - age 19-25',
  `conditionStatusId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'id from lu_MedicalConditionStatuses table',
  `conditionOrder` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'order for conditions - a continuous cough first, then lung cancer, etc.  Values will be 1, 2, 3',
  `comments` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'any additional information for the medical condition',
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT 'This is the date that the record was added to UT',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),

  KEY `mcIdFK_idx` (`conditionId`),
  KEY `mc_tranId_idx` (`transactionInId`),
  KEY `mcTypeFK_idx` (`conditionTypeId`),
  CONSTRAINT `mcIdFK` FOREIGN KEY (`conditionId`) REFERENCES `lu_medicalconditions` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `mcStatusId` FOREIGN KEY (`conditionStatusId`) REFERENCES `lu_medicalconditionstatuses` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `mcTypeFK` FOREIGN KEY (`conditionTypeId`) REFERENCES `message_medicalconditions` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `mc_tranId` FOREIGN KEY (`transactionInId`) REFERENCES `transactionin` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION

/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;

CREATE TABLE `message_medications` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `transactionInId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `sourceId` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'This is the id that the message source might have assigned to the record. For example, CCR components always has a CCRDataObjectId',
  `sourceDateType` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'The date type that the is provided with the record. It can be a date range, exact date, approximate date range, approximately age range, age range, verification date etc. ',
  `sourceDate` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'The date that the is provided with the record. e.g. exact time - Nov 11, 2011 11:11AM, age range - age 19-25',
  `manufacturerId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'id from lu_Manufacturers',
  `brandNameId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'id from lu_brandName',
  `medicationId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'look up from lu_Medications',
  `quantity` float DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'How much in total a patient should get of this medication e.g. 30',
  `quantityUnit` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'How much in total a patient should get of this medication e.g. capsules',

  `duration` float DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'how long should a patient take this  - e.g. 30',

  `directions` varchar(200) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'more specific directions - Stop taking if symptoms are gone.',
  `medGeneralStatusId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'past, current, future, etc.',
  `medOrder` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'If there are multiple medications for a message, specify the order medications of if needed.',

  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `medFK_idx` (`medicationId`),
  KEY `medStatusFK_idx` (`medGeneralStatusId`),
  KEY `meDManuFK_idx` (`manufacturerId`),
  KEY `medBrandNameFK_idx` (`brandNameId`),

  CONSTRAINT `medFK` FOREIGN KEY (`medicationId`) REFERENCES `lu_medications` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `meDManuFK` FOREIGN KEY (`manufacturerId`) REFERENCES `lu_manufacturers` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `med_tranId` FOREIGN KEY (`transactionInId`) REFERENCES `transactionin` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION

CREATE TABLE `message_patients` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT 'primary key for patient, it will serve as our system''s patient Id',
  `transactionInId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `sourcePatientId` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Id assigned to patient by source system - e.g Pat148R-2KD-BOS',
  `prefix` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. Mr, Dr., Ms, Sir, Princess, Knight, etc',
  `firstName` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. John',
  `middleName` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g Joshua',
  `lastName` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. Doe',
  `suffix` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. Jr, III, IV etc.',
  `dob` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Patient''s date of birth 1-1-1912',
  `genderId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Look up value from lu_Genders. Look up field is int and not free hand field because we should have some limits to some fields as what the user can type.  We will add it to our look up table if something creative comes up.  It is also a repetitive field, using int will take up less space and faster when it comes to indexing\nSample equivalent values are - male, female, unknown, transgender, etc.',
  `raceId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Look up Id from lu_Races - equivalent values could be Asian, White, Black, etc.',
  `hispanicId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'id from lu_Hispanics\nSample look up values are Yes, No, Not Reported',
  `primaryLanguageId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Id from lu_Languages - Sample look up values - English, Spanish, Polish, Mandarin (Chinese), Cantonese (Chinese) etc.',
  `englishProficient` varchar(10) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'can be Yes, No, Unknown...\nWe wi\nso changing it to varchar',
  `maritalStatusId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'look up from lu_MartialStatuses - Sample look up values are - Single, Married, Divorced, Not Reported, etc.',
  `initialContraceptiveId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `email` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. test@test.com',
  `additonalContactNumber` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL,
  `url` varchar(100) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'e.g. http://test.com',
  `occupation` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL,
  `guardianName` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'name of guardian - Jane Doe, John Smith',
  `emergencyContact` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'Name of emergency contact - Jane Doe',
  `emergencyTel` varchar(45) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '123-456-7890',
  `patientStatusId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL COMMENT 'id from lu_PatientStatuses - Could be equivalent int value of active, pending, future, expired, etc.',
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT 'This is the date that the record was added to UT',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `genderFK_idx` (`genderId`),
  KEY `raceFK_idx` (`raceId`),
  KEY `lauguageFK_idx` (`primaryLanguageId`),
  KEY `martialStatusFK_idx` (`maritalStatusId`),

  KEY `hispanicFK_idx` (`hispanicId`),
  KEY `contraFK_idx` (`initialContraceptiveId`),
  KEY `transFK_idx` (`transactionInId`),

  CONSTRAINT `genderFK` FOREIGN KEY (`genderId`) REFERENCES `lu_genders` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,

  CONSTRAINT `trTestTypeFK` FOREIGN KEY (`testResultId`) REFERENCES `lu_testresultstypes` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `tr_tranId` FOREIGN KEY (`transactionInId`) REFERENCES `transactionin` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION

DROP TABLE IF EXISTS `transactionouterrors`;
/*!40101 SET @saved_cs_client     = @@character_set_client */;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = utf8 */;
CREATE TABLE `transactionouterrors` (
  `id` int(11) NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT,
  `BatchDownloadId` int(11) NOT NULL,
  `transactionTargetId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `configId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `fieldNo` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `required` bit(1) DEFAULT NULL,
  `errorId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `cwId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `macroId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `validationTypeId` int(11) DEFAULT NULL,
  `stackTrace` text,
  `dateCreated` datetime NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  KEY `configFFIdFK_idx` (`fieldNo`),
  KEY `FKErrorId_idx` (`errorId`),
  KEY `validationTypeFKOut_idx` (`validationTypeId`),
  KEY `cwId_idx` (`cwId`),
  KEY `macroId_idx` (`macroId`),
  CONSTRAINT `cwIdFK` FOREIGN KEY (`cwId`) REFERENCES `crosswalks` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `errorIdFK` FOREIGN KEY (`errorId`) REFERENCES `lu_errorcodes` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `FKErrorId` FOREIGN KEY (`errorId`) REFERENCES `lu_errorcodes` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `macroIdFK` FOREIGN KEY (`macroId`) REFERENCES `macro_names` (`ID`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION,
  CONSTRAINT `validationTypeFKOut` FOREIGN KEY (`validationTypeId`) REFERENCES `ref_validationtypes` (`id`) ON DELETE NO ACTION ON UPDATE NO ACTION
) ENGINE=InnoDB DEFAULT CHARSET=latin1;
/*!40101 SET character_set_client = @saved_cs_client */;

/*!50003 DROP FUNCTION IF EXISTS `strSplit` */;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = utf8_general_ci */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_sql_mode       = @@sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = 'STRICT_TRANS_TABLES,NO_ENGINE_SUBSTITUTION' */ ;
DELIMITER ;;
CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` FUNCTION `strSplit`(x varchar(255), delim varchar(12), pos int) RETURNS varchar(255) CHARSET latin1
return replace(substring(substring_index(x, delim, pos), 
length(substring_index(x, delim, pos - 1)) + 1), delim, '') ;;
DELIMITER ;

/*!50003 DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS `addCharToString` */;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = utf8_general_ci */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_sql_mode       = @@sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = 'STRICT_TRANS_TABLES,NO_ENGINE_SUBSTITUTION' */ ;
DELIMITER ;;
CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `addCharToString`(in configId int, 
in batchId int, in srcField varchar(10),
in fieldA varchar(10), in fieldB varchar(10), in con1 varchar(10), 
in con2 varchar(10), in macroId int, in foroutboundProcessing boolean, in passClear int)
proc_main:begin

call setInboundOutBoundTables (foroutboundProcessing);
select @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable
into @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable;

call getFinalStatusIds;
select @finalStatusIds into @finalStatusIds;

-- we build sql here 
set @stmt = concat("update ", @translatedTable," set ",fieldA,
" = concat(substring(",fieldA,", 1,",con2,"-1), '",con1,"', substring(",fieldA,", ",con2,",(length(",fieldA,")))) where ", @transactionTable ,"Id in (select id from ",@transactionTable,
" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (",@finalStatusIds,"));");

PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
EXECUTE stmt;-- execute

-- we check pass /clear
if (passClear = 2) THEN
BEGIN
-- not sure how to pass clear this
END;
END IF;
-- see if we want to return something
select '';

end proc_main ;;
DELIMITER ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = @saved_sql_mode */ ;

/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = @saved_sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = @saved_cs_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = @saved_cs_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = @saved_col_connection */ ;
/*!50003 DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS `insertValidationErrors` */;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = utf8_general_ci */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_sql_mode       = @@sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = 'STRICT_TRANS_TABLES,NO_ENGINE_SUBSTITUTION' */ ;
DELIMITER ;;
CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `insertValidationErrors`(in vtType int, in fieldNo int,
in batchUploadId int, in configId int)
BEGIN

DECLARE regEx varchar(100) DEFAULT '';

CASE vtType
	WHEN 2 THEN set regEx = '^[A-Z0-9._%-]+@[A-Z0-9.-]+\.[A-Z]{2,4}$';
    WHEN 3 THEN 
		BEGIN 
			CALL `universalTranslator`.`stripPhoneChars`(vtType, fieldNo, batchUploadId, configId);
			set regEx ='^[0-9]{7,11}$';
		END;
	WHEN 5 THEN set regEx = '^-?[0-9]+[.]?[0-9]*$|^-?[.][0-9]+$';
    ELSE
        BEGIN
        END;
	END 
	CASE;
 
set @stmt = concat(
'insert into transactionInerrors (batchUploadId, transactionInId, fieldNo, errorid, 
validationTypeId) SELECT ', batchUploadId, ', transactionInId, ',fieldNo,',2, ', vtType,'  
 FROM transactionTranslatedIn WHERE F' ,fieldNo, ' not REGEXP  "', regEx, '" and F',fieldNo, ' is not null 
and length(F', fieldNO, ') != 0
and configId = ', configId, ' and transactionInId 
in (select id from transactionIn where batchId = ', batchUploadId,' and configId = ', configId,' and statusId != 12);');

PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
EXECUTE stmt;

 END ;;
DELIMITER ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = @saved_sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = @saved_cs_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = @saved_cs_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = @saved_col_connection */ ;
/*!50003 DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS `MatchFAUpdateSF` */;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = utf8_general_ci */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_sql_mode       = @@sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = 'STRICT_TRANS_TABLES,NO_ENGINE_SUBSTITUTION' */ ;
DELIMITER ;;
CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `MatchFAUpdateSF`(in configId int, 
in batchId int, in srcField varchar(10),
in fieldA varchar(10), in fieldB varchar(10), in con1 varchar(10), 
in con2 varchar(10), in macroId int, in foroutboundProcessing boolean, in passClear int)
proc_main:begin

-- this SP matches FieldA with Con1 and then updates fieldB with Con2
-- this sets out table
call setInboundOutBoundTables (foroutboundProcessing);
select @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable
into @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable;

call getFinalStatusIds;
select @finalStatusIds into @finalStatusIds;


-- build our sql
set @stmt = concat("update ",@translatedTable, " set ",srcField," = '",con2,"' where ",fieldA," = '",con1,"'
and ",@transactionTable,"Id in (select id from ",@transactionTable,
" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (", @finalStatusIds, "));");

PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
EXECUTE stmt;-- execute

-- we check pass /clear
if (passClear = 2) THEN
BEGIN
set @stmt = concat("update ",@translatedTable, " set ",srcField," = null where ",fieldB," != '",con2,"'
and ",@transactionTable,"Id in (select id from ",@transactionTable,
" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (", @finalStatusIds,"));");
PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
EXECUTE stmt;-- execute
END;
END IF;

-- the only error for this is if SP bombs, no need to write in insert error logs
select '';
end proc_main ;;
DELIMITER ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = @saved_sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = @saved_cs_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = @saved_cs_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = @saved_col_connection */ ;
/*!50003 DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS `MatchFieldAUpdateFieldB` */;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;

/*!50003 SET character_set_results = utf8 */ ;

CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `MatchFieldAUpdateFieldB`(in configId int, 
in batchId int, in srcField varchar(10),
in fieldA varchar(10), in fieldB varchar(10), in con1 varchar(10), 
in con2 varchar(10), in macroId int, in foroutboundProcessing boolean, in passClear int)
proc_main:begin

-- this SP matches FieldA with Con1 and then updates fieldB with Con2
-- this sets out table
call setInboundOutBoundTables (foroutboundProcessing);
select @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable
into @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable;

call getFinalStatusIds;
select @finalStatusIds into @finalStatusIds;


-- build our sql
set @stmt = concat("update ",@translatedTable, " set ",fieldB," = '",con2,"' where ",fieldA," = '",con1,"'
and ",@transactionTable,"Id in (select id from ",@transactionTable,
" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (",@finalStatusIds ,"));");

PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
EXECUTE stmt;-- execute

-- we check pass /clear
if (passClear = 2) THEN
BEGIN
set @stmt = concat("update ",@translatedTable, " set ",fieldB," = null where ",fieldB," != '",con2,"'
and ",@transactionTable,"Id in (select id from ",@transactionTable,
" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (",@finalStatusIds,"));");
PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
EXECUTE stmt;-- execute
END;
END IF;

-- the only error for this is if SP bombs, no need to write in insert error logs
select '';
end proc_main ;;
DELIMITER ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = @saved_sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = @saved_cs_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = @saved_cs_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = @saved_col_connection */ ;

CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `mmddyyyytoyyyymmdd`(in configId int, 
in batchId int, in srcField varchar(10),
in fieldA varchar(10), in fieldB varchar(10), in con1 varchar(10), 
in con2 varchar(10), in macroId int, in foroutboundProcessing boolean, in passClear int)
proc_main:begin

call setInboundOutBoundTables (foroutboundProcessing);
select @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable
into @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable;

call getFinalStatusIds;
select @finalStatusIds into @finalStatusIds;

if (length(fieldA) = 0) then
set fieldA = srcField;
end if;

if (length(con1) = 0) then
set con1 = "/";
end if;

-- we build sql here 
set @stmt = concat("update ", @translatedTable," set ",fieldA," = 
concat(substring(",srcField, ", 7,4), '",con1, "',  
substring(", srcField, ", 1,2),'",con1,"' ,substring(",srcField, ", 4,2))
where ", @transactionTable ,"Id in (select id from ",@transactionTable,
" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (", @finalStatusIds, "));");

PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
EXECUTE stmt;-- execute

-- we check pass /clear
if (passClear = 2) THEN
BEGIN
-- if we want to fail anything, we will set forcw to MACRO_ERROR
-- not sure how to pass clear this
END;
END IF;
-- see if we want to return something
select '';

end proc_main ;;
DELIMITER ;

CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `setFieldToNull`(in configId int, 
in batchId int, in srcField varchar(10),
in fieldA varchar(10), in fieldB varchar(10), in con1 varchar(10), 
in con2 varchar(10), in macroId int, in foroutboundProcessing boolean, in passClear int)
proc_main:begin

-- this SP matches FieldA with Con1 and then updates fieldB with Con2
-- this sets out table

into @translatedTable, @transactionTable, @batchTable, @batchIdType , @errorTable;

call getFinalStatusIds;
select @finalStatusIds into @finalStatusIds;


-- build our sql
set @stmt = concat("update ",@translatedTable, " set ",fieldA," = null where ");

if (fieldB != 'F') then 
set @stmt = concat(@stmt, fieldB," = '",con2,"' and ");
end if;

set @stmt =concat(@stmt, @transactionTable,"Id in (select id from ",@transactionTable,
" where configId = ",configId," and ", @batchIdType," = ",batchId," and statusId not in (",@finalStatusIds ,"));");

PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
EXECUTE stmt;-- execute

BEGIN

END;
END IF;

-- the only error for this is if SP bombs, no need to write in insert error logs

end proc_main ;;

CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `setInboundOutBoundTables`(in foroutboundProcessing boolean)
proc_main:begin

-- this SP sets the inbound / outbound tables
set @translatedTable = "transactionTranslatedIn";
set @transactionTable = "transactionIn";
set @batchTable = "batchUploads";
set @batchIdType = "batchId";
set @errorTable = "transactionInErrors";

if (foroutboundProcessing) THEN
BEGIN -- true
		set @translatedTable = "transactionTranslatedOut";
		set @transactionTable = "transactionTarget";
		set @batchTable = "batchDowloads";
		set @batchIdType = "batchDLId";
		set @errorTable = "transactionOutErrors";
END; 
END IF;

end proc_main ;;
DELIMITER ;

/*!50003 DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS `setSqlForConfig` */;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = utf8_general_ci */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_sql_mode       = @@sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = 'STRICT_TRANS_TABLES,NO_ENGINE_SUBSTITUTION' */ ;
DELIMITER ;;
CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `setSqlForConfig`(in inConfigId int, in batchUploadId int)
proc_main:begin
drop TEMPORARY TABLE if exists temp1;
CREATE TEMPORARY TABLE temp1
as (select min(fieldNo) as fieldNo, saveToTableName, savetotablecol, configId, batchUploadId
from configurationFormFields where configId = inConfigId
and saveToTableName != ''
group by savetotablecol, saveToTableName);
SELECT  batchUploadId, saveToTableName, 
group_concat(distinct savetotablecol ORDER BY fieldNo SEPARATOR ',') as savetotablecol,
group_concat( concat('F',fieldNo) ORDER BY fieldNo SEPARATOR ',') as singleValueFields, 
group_concat( concat('strSplit(F',fieldNo, ', ''^^^^^'',@valPos)') ORDER BY fieldNo SEPARATOR ',') as splitFields, 
group_concat( concat('F',fieldNo, ' like ''%^^^^^%''') ORDER BY fieldNo SEPARATOR ' or ') as checkForDelim,
configId
FROM temp1 
where configId = inConfigId
GROUP BY saveToTableName
ORDER BY saveToTableName;
end proc_main ;;
DELIMITER ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = @saved_sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = @saved_cs_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = @saved_cs_results */ ;

/*!50003 DROP PROCEDURE IF EXISTS `stripPhoneChars` */;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_client      = @@character_set_client */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_cs_results     = @@character_set_results */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_col_connection = @@collation_connection */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_client  = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET character_set_results = utf8 */ ;
/*!50003 SET collation_connection  = utf8_general_ci */ ;
/*!50003 SET @saved_sql_mode       = @@sql_mode */ ;
/*!50003 SET sql_mode              = 'STRICT_TRANS_TABLES,NO_ENGINE_SUBSTITUTION' */ ;
DELIMITER ;;
CREATE DEFINER=`root`@`localhost` PROCEDURE `stripPhoneChars`(in vtType int, in fieldNo int,
in batchUploadId int, in configId int)
BEGIN
	DECLARE varToReplace varchar(100) DEFAULT '.';
	DECLARE part1 varchar(255) DEFAULT '.';
	DECLARE part2 varchar(25) DEFAULT '.';

	set part1 = concat("update transactiontranslatedIn JOIN (SELECT id from transactionIn WHERE configId = ",
	  configId,"  and batchId = ", batchUploadId, ") as ti ON transactiontranslatedIn.transactionInId = ti.id SET transactiontranslatedIn.F"
	  , fieldNo, " = replace(F", fieldNo, ", '");
	set part2 = "', '');";
	set @stmt = concat(part1, varToReplace, part2);
  	PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt;

	set varToReplace = '-';
	set @stmt = concat(part1, varToReplace, part2);
	PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt;

	set varToReplace = ')';
	set @stmt = concat(part1, varToReplace, part2);
	PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt;

	set varToReplace = '(';
	set @stmt = concat(part1, varToReplace, part2);
	PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt;

	set varToReplace = ' ';
	set @stmt = concat(part1, varToReplace, part2);
	PREPARE stmt from @stmt;
	EXECUTE stmt;

 END ;;
DELIMITER ;
